2009-09-27 22:01:08.103 ljapp[96752:20b]  The Father and Son 'verses sprang from a slightly cracky idea which came up in an RP - what if Rille was Sabbat's father? Us being us, we picked it up and ran with it, and these were the result.
2009-09-27 22:01:08.104 ljapp[96752:20b] <br />
2009-09-27 22:01:08.105 ljapp[96752:20b] Open <br />
2009-09-27 22:01:08.105 ljapp[96752:20b] Close <br />
2009-09-27 22:01:08.107 ljapp[96752:20b] This one is an extension of all the other AUs - Rille and Sabbat are from Haiti, and are living in Some Big City Somewhere That Is Not In Haiti. Rille has a million and three jobs to keep their apartment, and Sabbat is having trouble at school. Not an assassin in sight. (*tear*)
